<pr_description>
[cli-tools-test] audit: tool usage parser extracts common English words as tool call names from agent logs
During daily CLI tools exploratory testing (run [§23632386989](https://github.com/github/gh-aw/actions/runs/23632386989)), a reproducible parsing bug was found in the `audit` tool's tool usage extraction logic.

### Problem Description

When the Copilot CLI agent's STDIO log contains natural language text that mentions tool-like words (e.g., "the agent **calls** a **command**"), the audit tool incorrectly extracts those words as tool call names. This contaminates the `tool_usage` report with English stop-words like `calls`, `call`, `to`, `for`, `or`, `on`, `with`, `since`, `launches`, `misuse`, `unified`, etc.

### Affected Run

- **Run ID**: [§23578198071](https://github.com/github/gh-aw/actions/runs/23578198071) — `GPL Dependency Cleaner (gpclean)`, `completed/failure`
- **Reproduced via**: `audit` MCP tool on this run ID

### Evidence

The `run_summary.json` → `metrics.ToolCalls` for this run contains:

````json
[
  {"Name": "calls",   "CallCount": 20, "MaxInputSize": 0, "MaxOutputSize": 0},
  {"Name": "call",    "CallCount": 5,  "MaxInputSize": 0, "MaxOutputSize": 0},
  {"Name": "to",      "CallCount": 3,  "MaxInputSize": 0, "MaxOutputSize": 0},
  {"Name": "or",      "CallCount": 1,  "MaxInputSize": 0, "MaxOutputSize": 0},
  {"Name": "for",     "CallCount": 1,  "MaxInputSize": 0, "MaxOutputSize": 0},
  {"Name": "on",      "CallCount": 1,  "MaxInputSize": 0, "MaxOutputSize": 0},
  {"Name": "since",   "CallCount": 2,  "MaxInputSize": 0, "MaxOutputSize": 0},
  {"Name": "with",    "CallCount": 1,  "MaxInputSize": 0, "MaxOutputSize": 0},
  {"Name": "misuse",  "CallCount": 1,  "MaxInputSize": 0, "MaxOutputSize": 0},
  {"Name": "unified", "CallCount": 1,  "MaxInputSize": 0, "MaxOutputSize": 0},
  {"Name": "launches","CallCount": 1,  "MaxInputSize": 0, "MaxOutputSize": 0},
  // REAL tools mixed in:
  {"Name": "startHttpServer", "CallCount": 1, ...},
  {"Name": "noop",            "CallCount": 1, ...},
  {"Name": "label_agent",     "CallCount": 1, ...}
]
```

Note: All false-positive entries have `MaxInputSize: 0` and `MaxOutputSize: 0`, unlike real tool calls which typically carry payloads.

The `ToolSequences` confirm the pattern — sequences like `["or", "calls", "call", "call", "call"]` and a 21-entry sequence of repeated `calls`/`since` clearly come from parsed natural language prose, not actual tool invocations.

### Downstream Impact

This bug causes cascading inaccuracies across the entire audit report:

| Field | Incorrect Value | Correct Value |
|-------|----------------|---------------|
| `behavior_fingerprint.tool_breadth` | `"broad"` (15 "tool types") | `"narrow"` (3 real tools) |
| `performance_metrics.most_used_tool` | `"calls (20 calls)"` | `"startHttpServer"` or `"noop"` |
| `observability_insights` | "The agent used 8 turns across **15 tool types**" | "...across **3 tool types**" |
| `comparison.delta` (other runs) | Baseline tool_breadth comparisons are wrong | — |

### Likely Root Cause

The parser extracting tool names from `agent-stdio.log` appears to use a regex or tokenizer that's too broad — it likely matches words near patterns like `● toolname` or `` ` toolname ` `` but also catches words in nearby context lines that are free text. The Copilot CLI log format uses `● toolname` for actual tool invocations, so the regex may need to be anchored more strictly to that exact prefix.

### Steps to Reproduce

```
Use the audit MCP tool with run_id_or_url: "23578198071"
Check tool_usage[] in the response — entries like "calls", "to", "for" are present
Compare with agent-stdio.log at /tmp/gh-aw/aw-mcp/logs/run-23578198071/agent-stdio.log
````

### Expected Behavior

`tool_usage` should only contain entries for actual tool invocations (e.g., `bash`, `edit`, `startHttpServer`, MCP tool names). English words from log prose should never appear as tool names.

### Actual Behavior

Common English words (`calls`, `call`, `to`, `for`, `on`, `or`, `with`, `since`, `launches`, `misuse`, `unified`) appear as tool names with call counts, polluting all downstream metrics.

### Environment

- **Repository**: github/gh-aw
- **Testing run**: [§23632386989](https://github.com/github/gh-aw/actions/runs/23632386989)
- **Date**: 2026-03-27
- **Affected runs confirmed**: 23578198071 (gpclean)

### Impact

- **Severity**: High
- **Frequency**: Affects any run where the Copilot CLI agent's log contains natural language that includes common verb-like words near the tool-call parsing window
- **Workaround**: None — the `tool_usage`, `behavior_fingerprint.tool_breadth`, and `most_used_tool` fields cannot be trusted for affected runs

**References:**
- [§23578198071](https://github.com/github/gh-aw/actions/runs/23578198071) — Affected run (gpclean failure)
- [§23632386989](https://github.com/github/gh-aw/actions/runs/23632386989) — Testing run that discovered this issue

    12	// SessionEntry represents a single entry in a Copilot session JSONL file
    13	type SessionEntry struct {
    14	        Type     string          `json:"type"`
    15	        Subtype  string          `json:"subtype,omitempty"`
    16	        Message  *SessionMessage `json:"message,omitempty"`
    17	        Usage    *SessionUsage   `json:"usage,omitempty"`
    18	        NumTurns int             `json:"num_turns,omitempty"`
    19	        RawData  map[string]any  `json:"-"`
    20	}

    24	        Content []SessionContent `json:"content"`
    25	}

    33	        Input     map[string]any `json:"input,omitempty"`

    36	}

    44	// parseSessionJSONL attempts to parse the log content as JSONL session format
    45	// Returns true if successful, false if the format is not recognized
    46	func (e *CopilotEngine) parseSessionJSONL(logContent string, verbose bool) (LogMetrics, bool) {
    47	        var metrics LogMetrics
    48	        var totalTokenUsage int
    49	        toolCallMap := make(map[string]*ToolCallInfo)
    50	        var currentSequence []string
    51	        turns := 0
    52	        assistantMessageCount := 0 // fallback: count assistant messages when num_turns is absent
    53	
    54	        lines := strings.Split(logContent, "\n")
    55	        foundSessionEntry := false
    56	
    57	        for _, line := range lines {
    58	                trimmedLine := strings.TrimSpace(line)
    59	
    60	                // Skip empty lines and debug log lines
    61	                if trimmedLine == "" || !strings.HasPrefix(trimmedLine, "{") {
    62	                        continue
    63	                }
    64	
    65	                // Try to parse as session entry
    66	                var entry SessionEntry
    67	                if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(trimmedLine), &entry); err != nil {
    68	                        continue
    69	                }
    70	
    71	                foundSessionEntry = true
    72	
    73	                // Handle different entry types
    74	                switch entry.Type {
    75	                case "system":
    76	                        // System init entry - no action needed for metrics
    77	                        if verbose {
    78	                                copilotLogsLog.Printf("Found system init entry")
    79	                        }
    80	
    81	                case "assistant":
    82	                        // Each assistant message represents one LLM turn
    83	                        assistantMessageCount++
    84	
    85	                        // Assistant message with potential tool calls
    86	                        if entry.Message != nil {
    87	                                for _, content := range entry.Message.Content {
    88	                                        if content.Type == "tool_use" {
    89	                                                toolName := content.Name
    90	
    91	                                                // Track in sequence
    92	                                                currentSequence = append(currentSequence, toolName)
    93	
    94	                                                // Calculate input size
    95	                                                inputSize := 0
    96	                                                if content.Input != nil {
    97	                                                        inputJSON, _ := json.Marshal(content.Input)
    98	                                                        inputSize = len(inputJSON)
    99	                                                }
   100	
   101	                                                // Update or create tool call info
   102	                                                if toolInfo, exists := toolCallMap[toolName]; exists {
   103	                                                        toolInfo.CallCount++
   104	                                                        if inputSize > toolInfo.MaxInputSize {
   105	                                                                toolInfo.MaxInputSize = inputSize
   106	                                                        }
   107	                                                } else {
   108	                                                        toolCallMap[toolName] = &ToolCallInfo{
   109	                                                                Name:          toolName,
   110	                                                                CallCount:     1,
   111	                                                                MaxInputSize:  inputSize,
   112	                                                                MaxOutputSize: 0,
   113	                                                        }
   114	                                                }
   115	
   116	                                                if verbose {
   117	                                                        copilotLogsLog.Printf("Found tool call: %s with input size %d", toolName, inputSize)
   118	                                                }
   119	                                        }
   120	                                }
   121	                        }
   122	
   123	                case "user":
   124	                        // User message with tool results
   125	                        if entry.Message != nil {
   126	                                for _, content := range entry.Message.Content {
   127	                                        if content.Type == "tool_result" && content.ToolUseID != "" {
   128	                                                // Track output size
   129	                                                outputSize := len(content.Content)
   130	
   131	                                                // Try to find the tool by matching recent tools in sequence
   132	                                                // Since we don't have the tool ID mapping, we'll update the most recent matching tool
   133	                                                for toolName, toolInfo := range toolCallMap {
   134	                                                        if outputSize > toolInfo.MaxOutputSize {
   135	                                                                toolInfo.MaxOutputSize = outputSize
   136	                                                                if verbose {
   137	                                                                        copilotLogsLog.Printf("Updated %s MaxOutputSize to %d bytes", toolName, outputSize)
   138	                                                                }
   139	                                                                break // Update first matching tool
   140	                                                        }
   141	                                                }
   142	                                        }
   143	                                }
   144	                        }
   145	
   146	                case "result":
   147	                        // Result entry with usage statistics
   148	                        if entry.Usage != nil {
   149	                                totalTokenUsage = entry.Usage.InputTokens + entry.Usage.OutputTokens
   150	                                turns = entry.NumTurns
   151	
   152	                                if verbose {
   153	                                        copilotLogsLog.Printf("Found result entry: input_tokens=%d, output_tokens=%d, num_turns=%d",
   154	                                                entry.Usage.InputTokens, entry.Usage.OutputTokens, turns)
   155	                                }
   156	                        }
   157	                }
   158	        }
   159	
   160	        // If turns was not set from num_turns (0 or absent), fall back to counting assistant messages.
   161	        // The Copilot CLI may omit num_turns from the result entry; each assistant message represents
   162	        // one LLM conversation turn.
   163	        if turns == 0 && assistantMessageCount > 0 {
   164	                turns = assistantMessageCount
   165	                copilotLogsLog.Printf("num_turns not available in result entry, using assistant message count as turns: %d", turns)
   166	        }
   167	
   168	        // If we found no session entries, return false to indicate fallback needed
   169	        if !foundSessionEntry {
   170	                return metrics, false
   171	        }
   172	
   173	        // Save current sequence before finalizing
   174	        if len(currentSequence) > 0 {
   175	                metrics.ToolSequences = append(metrics.ToolSequences, currentSequence)
   176	        }
   177	
   178	        // Finalize metrics
   179	        copilotLogsLog.Printf("Session JSONL parsing complete: totalTokenUsage=%d, turns=%d, toolCalls=%d",
   180	                totalTokenUsage, turns, len(toolCallMap))
   181	
   182	        FinalizeToolMetrics(FinalizeToolMetricsOptions{
   183	                Metrics:         &metrics,
   184	                ToolCallMap:     toolCallMap,
   185	                CurrentSequence: currentSequence,
   186	                Turns:           turns,
   187	                TokenUsage:      totalTokenUsage,
   188	        })
   189	
   190	        return metrics, true
   191	}

   193	// ParseLogMetrics implements engine-specific log parsing for Copilot CLI.
   194	//
   195	// Parsing Strategy:
   196	// 1. First attempts to parse as JSONL session format (from ~/.copilot/session-state/*.jsonl)
   197	// 2. Falls back to debug log format if JSONL parsing fails or finds no entries
   198	//
   199	// Token Counting Behavior:
   200	// Copilot CLI makes multiple API calls during a workflow run (one per turn).
   201	// Each API call returns a response with usage statistics including token counts.
   202	// This function accumulates token counts from ALL API responses to get the total
   203	// token usage for the entire workflow run.
   204	//
   205	// Example: If a run has 3 turns with token counts [1000, 1500, 800],
   206	// the total token usage will be 3300 (sum of all turns).
   207	//
   208	// This matches the behavior of the JavaScript parser in parse_copilot_log.cjs.
   209	func (e *CopilotEngine) ParseLogMetrics(logContent string, verbose bool) LogMetrics {
   210	        // Try parsing as JSONL session format first
   211	        if metrics, success := e.parseSessionJSONL(logContent, verbose); success {
   212	                copilotLogsLog.Printf("Successfully parsed session JSONL format")
   213	                return metrics
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        // Fall back to debug log format parsing
   217	        copilotLogsLog.Printf("JSONL parsing failed or no entries found, falling back to debug log format")
   218	
   219	        var metrics LogMetrics
   220	        var totalTokenUsage int
   221	
   222	        lines := strings.Split(logContent, "\n")
   223	        toolCallMap := make(map[string]*ToolCallInfo) // Track tool calls
   224	        var currentSequence []string                  // Track tool sequence
   225	        turns := 0
   226	
   227	        // Track multi-line JSON blocks for token extraction
   228	        var inDataBlock bool
   229	        var currentJSONLines []string
   230	
   231	        for _, line := range lines {
   232	                // Skip empty lines
   233	                if strings.TrimSpace(line) == "" {
   234	                        continue
   235	                }
   236	
   237	                // Detect start of a JSON data block from Copilot debug logs
   238	                // Format: "YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SS.sssZ [DEBUG] data:"
   239	                if strings.Contains(line, "[DEBUG] data:") {
   240	                        inDataBlock = true
   241	                        currentJSONLines = []string{}
   242	                        // Each API response data block represents one LLM conversation turn.
   243	                        // Copilot CLI debug logs don't have "User:"/"Human:" patterns, so we
   244	                        // count turns based on the number of API responses (data blocks).
   245	                        turns++
   246	                        // Save previous sequence before starting new turn
   247	                        if len(currentSequence) > 0 {
   248	                                metrics.ToolSequences = append(metrics.ToolSequences, currentSequence)
   249	                                currentSequence = []string{}
   250	                        }
   251	                        continue
   252	                }
   253	
   254	                // While in a data block, accumulate lines
   255	                if inDataBlock {
   256	                        // Check if this line has a timestamp (indicates it's a log line, not raw JSON)
   257	                        hasTimestamp := strings.Contains(line, "[DEBUG]")
   258	
   259	                        if hasTimestamp {
   260	                                // Strip the timestamp and [DEBUG] prefix to see what remains
   261	                                // Format: "YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SS.sssZ [DEBUG] {json content}"
   262	                                _, after, ok := strings.Cut(line, "[DEBUG]")
   263	                                if ok {
   264	                                        cleanLine := strings.TrimSpace(after) // Skip "[DEBUG]"
   265	
   266	                                        // If after stripping, the line starts with JSON characters, it's part of JSON
   267	                                        // Otherwise, it's a new log entry and we should end the block
   268	                                        if strings.HasPrefix(cleanLine, "{") || strings.HasPrefix(cleanLine, "}") ||
   269	                                                strings.HasPrefix(cleanLine, "[") || strings.HasPrefix(cleanLine, "]") ||
   270	                                                strings.HasPrefix(cleanLine, "\"") {
   271	                                                // This is JSON content - add it
   272	                                                currentJSONLines = append(currentJSONLines, cleanLine)
   273	                                        } else {
   274	                                                // This is a new log line (not JSON content) - end of JSON block
   275	                                                // Try to parse the accumulated JSON
   276	                                                if len(currentJSONLines) > 0 {
   277	                                                        jsonStr := strings.Join(currentJSONLines, "\n")
   278	                                                        copilotLogsLog.Printf("Parsing JSON block with %d lines (%d bytes)", len(currentJSONLines), len(jsonStr))
   279	                                                        jsonMetrics := ExtractJSONMetrics(jsonStr, verbose)
   280	                                                        // Accumulate token usage from all responses (not just max)
   281	                                                        // This matches the JavaScript parser behavior in parse_copilot_log.cjs
   282	                                                        if jsonMetrics.TokenUsage > 0 {
   283	                                                                copilotLogsLog.Printf("Extracted %d tokens from JSON block", jsonMetrics.TokenUsage)
   284	                                                                totalTokenUsage += jsonMetrics.TokenUsage
   285	                                                        } else {
   286	                                                                copilotLogsLog.Printf("No tokens extracted from JSON block (possible format issue)")
   287	                                                        }
   288	                                                        if jsonMetrics.EstimatedCost > 0 {
   289	                                                                metrics.EstimatedCost += jsonMetrics.EstimatedCost
   290	                                                        }
   291	
   292	                                                        // Extract tool call sizes from the JSON response
   293	                                                        e.extractToolCallSizes(jsonStr, toolCallMap, verbose)
   294	                                                }
   295	
   296	                                                inDataBlock = false
   297	                                                currentJSONLines = []string{}
   298	                                        }
   299	                                }
   300	                        } else {
   301	                                // Line has no timestamp - it's raw JSON, add it
   302	                                currentJSONLines = append(currentJSONLines, line)
   303	                        }
   304	                }
   305	
   306	                // Extract tool calls and add to sequence and toolCallMap
   307	                // "Executing tool: <name>" lines confirm tool execution and are used to populate
   308	                // both the tool sequence and tool call statistics. This handles the common case where
   309	                // Copilot CLI JSON blocks have empty tool_calls arrays but emit execution log lines.
   310	                if toolName := e.parseCopilotToolCallsWithSequence(line, toolCallMap); toolName != "" {
   311	                        currentSequence = append(currentSequence, toolName)
   312	                }
   313	        }
   314	
   315	        // Process any remaining JSON block at the end of file
   316	        if inDataBlock && len(currentJSONLines) > 0 {
   317	                jsonStr := strings.Join(currentJSONLines, "\n")
   318	                copilotLogsLog.Printf("Parsing final JSON block at EOF with %d lines (%d bytes)", len(currentJSONLines), len(jsonStr))
   319	                jsonMetrics := ExtractJSONMetrics(jsonStr, verbose)
   320	                // Accumulate token usage from all responses (not just max)
   321	                if jsonMetrics.TokenUsage > 0 {
   322	                        copilotLogsLog.Printf("Extracted %d tokens from final JSON block", jsonMetrics.TokenUsage)
   323	                        totalTokenUsage += jsonMetrics.TokenUsage
   324	                } else {
   325	                        copilotLogsLog.Printf("No tokens extracted from final JSON block (possible format issue)")
   326	                }
   327	                if jsonMetrics.EstimatedCost > 0 {
   328	                        metrics.EstimatedCost += jsonMetrics.EstimatedCost
   329	                }
   330	
   331	                // Extract tool call sizes from the JSON response
   332	                e.extractToolCallSizes(jsonStr, toolCallMap, verbose)
   333	        }
   334	
   335	        // Finalize metrics using shared helper
   336	        copilotLogsLog.Printf("Finalized metrics: totalTokenUsage=%d, turns=%d, toolCalls=%d", totalTokenUsage, turns, len(toolCallMap))
   337	        FinalizeToolMetrics(FinalizeToolMetricsOptions{
   338	                Metrics:         &metrics,
   339	                ToolCallMap:     toolCallMap,
   340	                CurrentSequence: currentSequence,
   341	                Turns:           turns,
   342	                TokenUsage:      totalTokenUsage,
   343	        })
   344	
   345	        return metrics
   346	}
   347	
   348	// extractToolCallSizes extracts tool call input and output sizes from Copilot JSON responses
   349	func (e *CopilotEngine) extractToolCallSizes(jsonStr string, toolCallMap map[string]*ToolCallInfo, verbose bool) {
   350	        // Try to parse the JSON string
   351	        var data map[string]any
   352	        if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(jsonStr), &data); err != nil {
   353	                if verbose {
   354	                        copilotLogsLog.Printf("Failed to parse JSON for tool size extraction: %v", err)
   355	                }
   356	                return
   357	        }
   358	
   359	        // Look for tool_calls in the choices array (Copilot/OpenAI format)
   360	        if choices, ok := data["choices"].([]any); ok {
   361	                for _, choice := range choices {
   362	                        if choiceMap, ok := choice.(map[string]any); ok {
   363	                                if message, ok := choiceMap["message"].(map[string]any); ok {
   364	                                        if toolCalls, ok := message["tool_calls"].([]any); ok {
   365	                                                e.processToolCalls(toolCalls, toolCallMap, verbose)
   366	                                        }
   367	                                }
   368	                        }
   369	                }
   370	        }
   371	
   372	        // Also check for tool_calls directly in the message (alternative format)
   373	        if message, ok := data["message"].(map[string]any); ok {
   374	                if toolCalls, ok := message["tool_calls"].([]any); ok {
   375	                        e.processToolCalls(toolCalls, toolCallMap, verbose)
   376	                }
   377	        }
   378	}
   379	
   380	// processToolCalls processes tool_calls array and updates tool call map with sizes
   381	func (e *CopilotEngine) processToolCalls(toolCalls []any, toolCallMap map[string]*ToolCallInfo, verbose bool) {
   382	        for _, toolCall := range toolCalls {
   383	                if tcMap, ok := toolCall.(map[string]any); ok {
   384	                        // Extract function information
   385	                        if function, ok := tcMap["function"].(map[string]any); ok {
   386	                                if toolName, ok := function["name"].(string); ok {
   387	                                        // Calculate input size from arguments (if present)
   388	                                        inputSize := 0
   389	                                        if arguments, ok := function["arguments"].(string); ok {
   390	                                                inputSize = len(arguments)
   391	                                        }
   392	
   393	                                        // Initialize or update tool call info
   394	                                        if toolInfo, exists := toolCallMap[toolName]; exists {
   395	                                                toolInfo.CallCount++
   396	                                                // Update max input size if this call is larger
   397	                                                if inputSize > toolInfo.MaxInputSize {
   398	                                                        toolInfo.MaxInputSize = inputSize
   399	                                                        if verbose {
   400	                                                                copilotLogsLog.Printf("Updated %s MaxInputSize to %d bytes", toolName, inputSize)
   401	                                                        }
   402	                                                }
   403	                                        } else {
   404	                                                toolCallMap[toolName] = &ToolCallInfo{
   405	                                                        Name:          toolName,
   406	                                                        CallCount:     1,
   407	                                                        MaxInputSize:  inputSize,
   408	                                                        MaxOutputSize: 0, // Output size extraction not yet available in Copilot logs
   409	                                                }
   410	                                                if verbose {
   411	                                                        copilotLogsLog.Printf("Created tool info for %s with MaxInputSize=%d bytes", toolName, inputSize)
   412	                                                }
   413	                                        }
   414	                                }
   415	                        }
   416	                }
   417	        }
   418	}
   419	
   420	// parseCopilotToolCallsWithSequence extracts tool call information from Copilot CLI log lines and returns tool name.
   421	// It also updates toolCallMap with the tool execution count for statistics tracking.
   422	func (e *CopilotEngine) parseCopilotToolCallsWithSequence(line string, toolCallMap map[string]*ToolCallInfo) string {
   423	        // Look for "Executing tool:" pattern in Copilot logs
   424	        if strings.Contains(line, "Executing tool:") {
   425	                // Extract tool name from "Executing tool: <name>" format
   426	                parts := strings.Split(line, "Executing tool:")
   427	                if len(parts) > 1 {
   428	                        toolName := strings.TrimSpace(parts[1])
   429	                        if toolName == "" {
   430	                                return ""
   431	                        }
   432	                        // Update toolCallMap: this captures tool calls from execution log lines.
   433	                        // This is the primary source of tool call data in the Copilot CLI debug log
   434	                        // format, since JSON response blocks often have empty tool_calls arrays.
   435	                        if toolInfo, exists := toolCallMap[toolName]; exists {
   436	                                toolInfo.CallCount++
   437	                        } else {
   438	                                toolCallMap[toolName] = &ToolCallInfo{
   439	                                        Name:      toolName,
   440	                                        CallCount: 1,
   441	                                }
   442	                        }
   443	                        return toolName
   444	                }
   445	        }
   446	
   447	        return ""
   448	}
   449	
   450	// GetLogParserScriptId returns the JavaScript script name for parsing Copilot logs
   451	func (e *CopilotEngine) GetLogParserScriptId() string {
   452	        return "parse_copilot_log"
   453	}

    10	var (
    11	        agentTurnPattern     = regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)task.*iteration|agent.*turn|step.*\d+`)
    12	        agentToolCallPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)tool.*call|executing.*tool|calling.*(\w+)`)
    13	        toolNamePatterns     = []*regexp.Regexp{
    14	                regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)tool[:\s]+([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)`),
    15	                regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)calling[:\s]+([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)`),
    16	                regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)executing[:\s]+([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)`),

    18	        }

    21	// ParseCopilotCodingAgentLogMetrics extracts metrics from GitHub Copilot coding agent logs
    22	// This is different from Copilot CLI logs and requires specialized parsing
    23	func ParseCopilotCodingAgentLogMetrics(logContent string, verbose bool) workflow.LogMetrics {
    24	        copilotCodingAgentLog.Printf("Parsing GitHub Copilot coding agent log metrics: %d bytes", len(logContent))
    25	
    26	        var metrics workflow.LogMetrics
    27	        var maxTokenUsage int
    28	
    29	        lines := strings.Split(logContent, "\n")
    30	        toolCallMap := make(map[string]*workflow.ToolCallInfo)
    31	        var currentSequence []string
    32	        turns := 0
    33	
    34	        for _, line := range lines {
    35	                // Skip empty lines
    36	                if strings.TrimSpace(line) == "" {
    37	                        continue
    38	                }
    39	
    40	                // Count turns based on agent iteration patterns
    41	                if agentTurnPattern.MatchString(line) {
    42	                        turns++
    43	                        // Start of a new turn, save previous sequence if any
    44	                        if len(currentSequence) > 0 {
    45	                                metrics.ToolSequences = append(metrics.ToolSequences, currentSequence)
    46	                                currentSequence = []string{}
    47	                        }
    48	                }
    49	
    50	                // Extract tool calls from agent logs
    51	                if matches := agentToolCallPattern.FindStringSubmatch(line); len(matches) > 1 {
    52	                        toolName := extractToolName(line)
    53	                        if toolName != "" {
    54	                                // Track tool call
    55	                                if _, exists := toolCallMap[toolName]; !exists {
    56	                                        toolCallMap[toolName] = &workflow.ToolCallInfo{
    57	                                                Name:      toolName,
    58	                                                CallCount: 0,
    59	                                        }
    60	                                }
    61	                                toolCallMap[toolName].CallCount++
    62	
    63	                                // Add to current sequence
    64	                                currentSequence = append(currentSequence, toolName)
    65	
    66	                                if verbose {
    67	                                        copilotCodingAgentLog.Printf("Found tool call: %s", toolName)
    68	                                }
    69	                        }
    70	                }
    71	
    72	                // Try to extract token usage from JSON format if available
    73	                jsonMetrics := workflow.ExtractJSONMetrics(line, verbose)
    74	                if jsonMetrics.TokenUsage > 0 || jsonMetrics.EstimatedCost > 0 {
    75	                        if jsonMetrics.TokenUsage > maxTokenUsage {
    76	                                maxTokenUsage = jsonMetrics.TokenUsage
    77	                        }
    78	                        if jsonMetrics.EstimatedCost > 0 {
    79	                                metrics.EstimatedCost += jsonMetrics.EstimatedCost
    80	                        }
    81	                }
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        // Add final sequence if any
    85	        if len(currentSequence) > 0 {
    86	                metrics.ToolSequences = append(metrics.ToolSequences, currentSequence)
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        // Convert tool call map to slice
    90	        for _, toolInfo := range toolCallMap {
    91	                metrics.ToolCalls = append(metrics.ToolCalls, *toolInfo)
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        metrics.TokenUsage = maxTokenUsage
    95	        metrics.Turns = turns
    96	
    97	        copilotCodingAgentLog.Printf("Parsed metrics: tokens=%d, cost=$%.4f, turns=%d",
    98	                metrics.TokenUsage, metrics.EstimatedCost, metrics.Turns)
    99	
   100	        return metrics
   101	}
   102	
   103	// extractToolName extracts a tool name from a log line
   104	func extractToolName(line string) string {
   105	        // Try to extract tool name from various patterns
   106	        for _, pattern := range toolNamePatterns {
   107	                if matches := pattern.FindStringSubmatch(line); len(matches) > 1 {
   108	                        return strings.TrimSpace(matches[1])
   109	                }
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        return ""
   113	}

     1	// This file provides command-line interface functionality for gh-aw.
     2	// This file (logs_parsing_core.go) contains core log parsing functions
     3	// for locating and extracting engine configuration from workflow logs.
     4	//
     5	// Key responsibilities:
     6	//   - Parsing aw_info.json to extract engine configuration
     7	//   - Locating agent log files and output artifacts
     8	//   - Supporting multiple artifact layouts (before/after flattening)
     9	
    10	package cli
    11	
    12	import (
    13	        "encoding/json"
    14	        "errors"
    15	        "fmt"
    16	        "os"
    17	        "path/filepath"
    18	        "strings"
    19	
    20	        "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/console"
    21	        "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/constants"
    22	        "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/fileutil"
    23	        "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/logger"
    24	        "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/workflow"
    25	)
    26	
    27	var logsParsingCoreLog = logger.New("cli:logs_parsing_core")
    28	
    29	// parseAwInfo reads and parses aw_info.json file, returning the parsed data
    30	// Handles cases where aw_info.json is a file or a directory containing the actual file
    31	func parseAwInfo(infoFilePath string, verbose bool) (*AwInfo, error) {
    32	        // Sanitize the path to prevent path traversal attacks
    33	        cleanPath := filepath.Clean(infoFilePath)
    34	        logsParsingCoreLog.Printf("Parsing aw_info.json from: %s", cleanPath)
    35	        var data []byte
    36	        var err error
    37	
    38	        // Check if the path exists and determine if it's a file or directory
    39	        stat, statErr := os.Stat(cleanPath)
    40	        if statErr != nil {
    41	                logsParsingCoreLog.Printf("Failed to stat aw_info.json: %v", statErr)
    42	                if verbose {
    43	                        fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatWarningMessage(fmt.Sprintf("Failed to stat aw_info.json: %v", statErr)))
    44	                }
    45	                return nil, statErr
    46	        }
    47	
    48	        if stat.IsDir() {
    49	                // It's a directory - look for nested aw_info.json
    50	                nestedPath := filepath.Join(cleanPath, "aw_info.json")
    51	                if verbose {
    52	                        fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatInfoMessage("aw_info.json is a directory, trying nested file: "+nestedPath))
    53	                }
    54	                data, err = os.ReadFile(nestedPath)
    55	        } else {
    56	                // It's a regular file
    57	                data, err = os.ReadFile(cleanPath)
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        if err != nil {
    61	                if verbose {
    62	                        fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatWarningMessage(fmt.Sprintf("Failed to read aw_info.json: %v", err)))
    63	                }
    64	                return nil, err
    65	        }
    66	
    67	        var info AwInfo
    68	        if err := json.Unmarshal(data, &info); err != nil {
    69	                logsParsingCoreLog.Printf("Failed to unmarshal aw_info.json: %v", err)
    70	                if verbose {
    71	                        fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatWarningMessage(fmt.Sprintf("Failed to parse aw_info.json: %v", err)))
    72	                }
    73	                return nil, err
    74	        }
    75	
    76	        logsParsingCoreLog.Printf("Successfully parsed aw_info.json with engine_id: %s", info.EngineID)
    77	        return &info, nil
    78	}
    79	
    80	// extractEngineFromAwInfo reads aw_info.json and returns the appropriate engine
    81	// Handles cases where aw_info.json is a file or a directory containing the actual file
    82	func extractEngineFromAwInfo(infoFilePath string, verbose bool) workflow.CodingAgentEngine {
    83	        logsParsingCoreLog.Printf("Extracting engine from aw_info.json: %s", infoFilePath)
    84	        info, err := parseAwInfo(infoFilePath, verbose)
    85	        if err != nil {
    86	                return nil
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        if info.EngineID == "" {
    90	                logsParsingCoreLog.Print("No engine_id found in aw_info.json")
    91	                if verbose {
    92	                        fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatWarningMessage("No engine_id found in aw_info.json"))
    93	                }
    94	                return nil
    95	        }
    96	
    97	        registry := workflow.GetGlobalEngineRegistry()
    98	        engine, err := registry.GetEngine(info.EngineID)
    99	        if err != nil {
   100	                logsParsingCoreLog.Printf("Unknown engine: %s", info.EngineID)
   101	                if verbose {
   102	                        fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatWarningMessage("Unknown engine in aw_info.json: "+info.EngineID))
   103	                }
   104	                return nil
   105	        }
   106	
   107	        logsParsingCoreLog.Printf("Successfully extracted engine: %s", engine.GetID())
   108	        return engine
   109	}
   110	
   111	// findAgentOutputFile searches for a file named agent_output.json within the logDir tree.
   112	// Returns the first path found (depth-first) and a boolean indicating success.
   113	func findAgentOutputFile(logDir string) (string, bool) {
   114	        var foundPath string
   115	        _ = filepath.Walk(logDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
   116	                if err != nil || info == nil {
   117	                        return nil
   118	                }
   119	                if !info.IsDir() && strings.EqualFold(info.Name(), constants.AgentOutputArtifactName) {
   120	                        foundPath = path
   121	                        return errors.New("stop") // sentinel to stop walking early
   122	                }
   123	                return nil
   124	        })
   125	        if foundPath == "" {
   126	                return "", false
   127	        }
   128	        return foundPath, true
   129	}
   130	
   131	// findAgentLogFile searches for agent logs within the logDir.
   132	// It uses engine.GetLogFileForParsing() to determine which log file to use:
   133	//   - If GetLogFileForParsing() returns a non-empty value that doesn't point to agent-stdio.log,
   134	//     look for files in the "agent_output" artifact directory (before flattening)
   135	//     or in the flattened location (after flattening)
   136	//   - Otherwise, look for the "agent-stdio.log" artifact file
   137	//
   138	// Returns the first path found and a boolean indicating success.
   139	func findAgentLogFile(logDir string, engine workflow.CodingAgentEngine) (string, bool) {
   140	        // Use GetLogFileForParsing to determine which log file to use
   141	        logFileForParsing := engine.GetLogFileForParsing()
   142	
   143	        // If the engine specifies a log file that isn't the default agent-stdio.log,
   144	        // look in the agent_output artifact directory or flattened location
   145	        if logFileForParsing != "" && logFileForParsing != defaultAgentStdioLogPath {
   146	                // Check for agent_output directory (artifact, before flattening)
   147	                agentOutputDir := filepath.Join(logDir, "agent_output")
   148	                if fileutil.DirExists(agentOutputDir) {
   149	                        // Find the first file in this directory
   150	                        var foundFile string
   151	                        _ = filepath.Walk(agentOutputDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
   152	                                if err != nil || info == nil {
   153	                                        return nil
   154	                                }
   155	                                if !info.IsDir() && foundFile == "" {
   156	                                        foundFile = path
   157	                                        return errors.New("stop") // sentinel to stop walking early
   158	                                }
   159	                                return nil
   160	                        })
   161	                        if foundFile != "" {
   162	                                return foundFile, true
   163	                        }
   164	                }
   165	
   166	                // Check for flattened location (after flattening)
   167	                // The engine's log path is absolute (e.g., /tmp/gh-aw/sandbox/agent/logs/)
   168	                // After flattening, it's at logDir/sandbox/agent/logs/
   169	                // Strip /tmp/gh-aw/ prefix to get the relative path
   170	                const tmpGhAwPrefix = "/tmp/gh-aw/"
   171	                if after, ok := strings.CutPrefix(logFileForParsing, tmpGhAwPrefix); ok {
   172	                        relPath := after
   173	                        flattenedDir := filepath.Join(logDir, relPath)
   174	                        logsParsingCoreLog.Printf("Checking flattened location for logs: %s", flattenedDir)
   175	                        if fileutil.DirExists(flattenedDir) {
   176	                                // Find the first .log file in this directory
   177	                                var foundFile string
   178	                                _ = filepath.Walk(flattenedDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
   179	                                        if err != nil || info == nil {
   180	                                                return nil
   181	                                        }
   182	                                        if !info.IsDir() && strings.HasSuffix(info.Name(), ".log") && foundFile == "" {
   183	                                                foundFile = path
   184	                                                logsParsingCoreLog.Printf("Found session log file: %s", path)
   185	                                                return errors.New("stop") // sentinel to stop walking early
   186	                                        }
   187	                                        return nil
   188	                                })
   189	                                if foundFile != "" {
   190	                                        return foundFile, true
   191	                                }
   192	                        }
   193	                }
   194	
   195	                // Fallback: search recursively in logDir for session*.log or process*.log files
   196	                // This handles cases where the artifact structure is different than expected
   197	                // Note: Copilot changed from session-*.log to process-*.log naming convention
   198	                logsParsingCoreLog.Printf("Searching recursively in %s for session*.log or process*.log files", logDir)
   199	                var foundFile string
   200	                _ = filepath.Walk(logDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
   201	                        if err != nil || info == nil {
   202	                                return nil
   203	                        }
   204	                        // Look for session*.log or process*.log files
   205	                        fileName := info.Name()
   206	                        if !info.IsDir() && (strings.HasPrefix(fileName, "session") || strings.HasPrefix(fileName, "process")) && strings.HasSuffix(fileName, ".log") && foundFile == "" {
   207	                                foundFile = path
   208	                                logsParsingCoreLog.Printf("Found Copilot log file via recursive search: %s", path)
   209	                                return errors.New("stop") // sentinel to stop walking early
   210	                        }
   211	                        return nil
   212	                })
   213	                if foundFile != "" {
   214	                        return foundFile, true
   215	                }
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        // Default to agent-stdio.log
   219	        agentStdioLog := filepath.Join(logDir, "agent-stdio.log")
   220	        if fileutil.FileExists(agentStdioLog) {
   221	                return agentStdioLog, true
   222	        }
   223	
   224	        // Also check for nested agent-stdio.log in case it's in a subdirectory
   225	        var foundPath string
   226	        _ = filepath.Walk(logDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
   227	                if err != nil || info == nil {
   228	                        return nil
   229	                }
   230	                if !info.IsDir() && info.Name() == "agent-stdio.log" {
   231	                        foundPath = path
   232	                        return errors.New("stop") // sentinel to stop walking early
   233	                }
   234	                return nil
   235	        })
   236	        if foundPath != "" {
   237	                return foundPath, true
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        return "", false
   241	}
   242

     2	// This file (logs_parsing_engines.go) contains engine-specific log parsing
     3	// functionality for various AI engines (Claude, Copilot, Codex, Custom).
     4	//
     5	// Key responsibilities:
     6	//   - Parsing log files using engine-specific parsers
     7	//   - Detecting and parsing GitHub Copilot coding agent logs
     8	//   - Falling back to generic parser when engine is unknown
     9	
    10	package cli
    11	
    12	import (
    13	        "fmt"
    14	        "os"
    15	
    16	        "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/console"
    17	        "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/logger"

    20	
    21	var logsParsingEnginesLog = logger.New("cli:logs_parsing_engines")
    22	
    23	// parseLogFileWithEngine parses a log file using a specific engine or falls back to auto-detection
    24	func parseLogFileWithEngine(filePath string, detectedEngine workflow.CodingAgentEngine, isGitHubCopilotCodingAgent bool, verbose bool) (LogMetrics, error) {
    25	        logsParsingEnginesLog.Printf("Parsing log file: %s, isGitHubCopilotCodingAgent=%v", filePath, isGitHubCopilotCodingAgent)
    26	        // Read the entire log file at once to avoid JSON parsing issues from chunked reading
    27	        content, err := os.ReadFile(filePath)
    28	        if err != nil {
    29	                logsParsingEnginesLog.Printf("Failed to read log file: %v", err)
    30	                return LogMetrics{}, fmt.Errorf("error reading log file: %w", err)
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        logContent := string(content)
    34	        logsParsingEnginesLog.Printf("Read %d bytes from log file", len(logContent))
    35	
    36	        // If this is a GitHub Copilot coding agent run, use the specialized parser
    37	        if isGitHubCopilotCodingAgent {
    38	                logsParsingEnginesLog.Print("Using GitHub Copilot coding agent parser")
    39	                return ParseCopilotCodingAgentLogMetrics(logContent, verbose), nil
    40	        }
    41	
    42	        // If we have a detected engine from aw_info.json, use it directly
    43	        if detectedEngine != nil {
    44	                logsParsingEnginesLog.Printf("Using detected engine: %s", detectedEngine.GetID())
    45	                return detectedEngine.ParseLogMetrics(logContent, verbose), nil
    46	        }
    47	
    48	        // No aw_info.json metadata available - use fallback parser with common error patterns
    49	        logsParsingEnginesLog.Print("No engine detected, using fallback parser with common error patterns")
    50	        if verbose {
    51	                fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatWarningMessage("No aw_info.json found, using fallback parser"))
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        // Use empty metrics for fallback case
    55	        var metrics LogMetrics
    56	
    57	        return metrics, nil
    58	}

func extractToolName(line string) string {
        candidates := []string{strings.TrimSpace(line)}
        if _, message, ok := strings.Cut(line, "]"); ok {
                candidates = append(candidates, strings.TrimSpace(message))
        }
        if _, message, ok := strings.Cut(line, ":"); ok {
                candidates = append(candidates, strings.TrimSpace(message))
        }

        // Try to extract tool name from explicit invocation patterns only.
        for _, candidate := range candidates {
                for _, pattern := range toolNamePatterns {
                        if matches := pattern.FindStringSubmatch(candidate); len(matches) > 1 {
                                return strings.TrimSpace(matches[1])
                        }
                }
        }

        return ""
}

    10	var (
    11	        agentTurnPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)task.*iteration|agent.*turn|step.*\d+`)
    12	        toolNamePatterns = []*regexp.Regexp{
    13	                // Copilot CLI renders actual tool invocations with a leading bullet.
    14	                regexp.MustCompile(`^\s*●\s*([a-zA-Z0-9_.-]+)\b`),
    15	                // Keep support for explicit structured log lines, but require the
    16	                // invocation marker at the start of the (possibly prefix-stripped)
    17	                // log message and a delimiter.  Broad patterns like "tool.*call" or
    18	                // "calling.*" match ordinary prose such as "the tool calls parser".
    19	                regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)^\s*tool\s+call\s*:\s*([a-zA-Z0-9_.-]+)\b`),
    20	                regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)^\s*calling\s*:\s*([a-zA-Z0-9_.-]+)\b`),
    21	                regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)^\s*executing\s*:\s*([a-zA-Z0-9_.-]+)\b`),
    22	                regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)^\s*executing\s+tool\s*:\s*([a-zA-Z0-9_.-]+)\b`),
    23	                regexp.MustCompile(`(?i)^\s*using\s+tool\s*:\s*([a-zA-Z0-9_.-]+)\b`),
    24	        }
    25	)
    26	
    27	// ParseCopilotCodingAgentLogMetrics extracts metrics from GitHub Copilot coding agent logs
    28	// This is different from Copilot CLI logs and requires specialized parsing
    29	func ParseCopilotCodingAgentLogMetrics(logContent string, verbose bool) workflow.LogMetrics {
    30	        copilotCodingAgentLog.Printf("Parsing GitHub Copilot coding agent log metrics: %d bytes", len(logContent))
    31	
    32	        var metrics workflow.LogMetrics
    33	        var maxTokenUsage int
    34	
    35	        lines := strings.Split(logContent, "\n")
    36	        toolCallMap := make(map[string]*workflow.ToolCallInfo)
    37	        var currentSequence []string
    38	        turns := 0
    39	
    40	        for _, line := range lines {
    41	                // Skip empty lines
    42	                if strings.TrimSpace(line) == "" {
    43	                        continue
    44	                }
    45	
    46	                // Count turns based on agent iteration patterns
    47	                if agentTurnPattern.MatchString(line) {
    48	                        turns++
    49	                        // Start of a new turn, save previous sequence if any
    50	                        if len(currentSequence) > 0 {
    51	                                metrics.ToolSequences = append(metrics.ToolSequences, currentSequence)
    52	                                currentSequence = []string{}
    53	                        }
    54	                }
    55	
    56	                // Extract tool calls from agent logs.  Only explicit invocation
    57	                // lines are considered; natural language containing words like
    58	                // "tool", "calls", or "calling" must not produce tool usage.
    59	                toolName := extractToolName(line)
    60	                if toolName != "" {
    61	                        // Track tool call
    62	                        if _, exists := toolCallMap[toolName]; !exists {
    63	                                toolCallMap[toolName] = &workflow.ToolCallInfo{
    64	                                        Name:      toolName,
    65	                                        CallCount: 0,
    66	                                }
    67	                        }
    68	                        toolCallMap[toolName].CallCount++
    69	
    70	                        // Add to current sequence
    71	                        currentSequence = append(currentSequence, toolName)
    72	
    73	                        if verbose {
    74	                                copilotCodingAgentLog.Printf("Found tool call: %s", toolName)
    75	                        }
    76	                }
    77	
    78	                // Try to extract token usage from JSON format if available
    79	                jsonMetrics := workflow.ExtractJSONMetrics(line, verbose)
    80	                if jsonMetrics.TokenUsage > 0 || jsonMetrics.EstimatedCost > 0 {
    81	                        if jsonMetrics.TokenUsage > maxTokenUsage {
    82	                                maxTokenUsage = jsonMetrics.TokenUsage
    83	                        }
    84	                        if jsonMetrics.EstimatedCost > 0 {
    85	                                metrics.EstimatedCost += jsonMetrics.EstimatedCost
    86	                        }
    87	                }
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        // Add final sequence if any
    91	        if len(currentSequence) > 0 {
    92	                metrics.ToolSequences = append(metrics.ToolSequences, currentSequence)
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        // Convert tool call map to slice
    96	        for _, toolInfo := range toolCallMap {
    97	                metrics.ToolCalls = append(metrics.ToolCalls, *toolInfo)
    98	        }
    99	
   100	        metrics.TokenUsage = maxTokenUsage
   101	        metrics.Turns = turns
   102	
   103	        copilotCodingAgentLog.Printf("Parsed metrics: tokens=%d, cost=$%.4f, turns=%d",
   104	                metrics.TokenUsage, metrics.EstimatedCost, metrics.Turns)
   105	
   106	        return metrics
   107	}
   108	
   109	// extractToolName extracts a tool name from a log line
   110	func extractToolName(line string) string {
   111	        candidates := []string{strings.TrimSpace(line)}
   112	        if _, message, ok := strings.Cut(line, "]"); ok {
   113	                candidates = append(candidates, strings.TrimSpace(message))
   114	        }
   115	        if _, message, ok := strings.Cut(line, ":"); ok {
   116	                candidates = append(candidates, strings.TrimSpace(message))
   117	        }
   118	
   119	        // Try to extract tool name from explicit invocation patterns only.
   120	        for _, candidate := range candidates {
   121	                for _, pattern := range toolNamePatterns {
   122	                        if matches := pattern.FindStringSubmatch(candidate); len(matches) > 1 {
   123	                                return strings.TrimSpace(matches[1])
   124	                        }
   125	                }
   126	        }
   127	
   128	        return ""
   129	}

    13	/**
    14	 * Extracts the premium request count from the log content using regex
    15	 * @param {string} logContent - The raw log content as a string
    16	 * @returns {number} The number of premium requests consumed (defaults to 1 if not found)
    17	 */
    18	function extractPremiumRequestCount(logContent) {
    19	  // Try various patterns that might appear in the Copilot CLI output
    20	  // Use \d+(?:\.\d+)? to match both integers and decimals (e.g., 1, 0.33, 2.5)
    21	  const patterns = [/premium\s+requests?\s+consumed:?\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/i, /(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s+premium\s+requests?\s+consumed/i, /consumed\s+(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s+premium\s+requests?/i];
    22	
    23	  for (const pattern of patterns) {
    24	    const match = logContent.match(pattern);
    25	    if (match && match[1]) {
    26	      const count = parseFloat(match[1]);
    27	      if (!isNaN(count) && count > 0) {
    28	        return count;
    29	      }
    30	    }
    31	  }
    32	
    33	  // Default to 1 if no match found
    34	  // For agentic workflows, 1 premium request is consumed per workflow run
    35	  return 1;
    36	}
    37	
    38	/**
    39	 * Parses Copilot CLI log content and converts it to markdown format
    40	 * @param {string} logContent - The raw log content as a string
    41	 * @returns {{markdown: string, logEntries: Array, mcpFailures?: string[], maxTurnsHit?: boolean}} Formatted result with markdown and metadata
    42	 */
    43	function parseCopilotLog(logContent) {
    44	  let logEntries;
    45	
    46	  // First, try to parse as JSON array (structured format)
    47	  try {
    48	    logEntries = JSON.parse(logContent);
    49	    if (!Array.isArray(logEntries)) {
    50	      throw new Error(`${ERR_PARSE}: Not a JSON array`);
    51	    }
    52	  } catch (jsonArrayError) {
    53	    // If that fails, try to parse as debug logs format
    54	    const debugLogEntries = parseDebugLogFormat(logContent);
    55	    if (debugLogEntries && debugLogEntries.length > 0) {
    56	      logEntries = debugLogEntries;
    57	    } else {
    58	      // Try JSONL format using shared function
    59	      logEntries = parseLogEntries(logContent);
    60	    }
    61	  }
    62	
    63	  if (!logEntries || logEntries.length === 0) {
    64	    return { markdown: "## Agent Log Summary\n\nLog format not recognized as Copilot JSON array or JSONL.\n", logEntries: [] };
    65	  }
    66	
    67	  // Generate conversation markdown using shared function
    68	  const conversationResult = generateConversationMarkdown(logEntries, {
    69	    formatToolCallback: (toolUse, toolResult) => formatToolUse(toolUse, toolResult, { includeDetailedParameters: true }),
    70	    formatInitCallback: initEntry =>
    71	      formatInitializationSummary(initEntry, {
    72	        includeSlashCommands: false,
    73	        modelInfoCallback: entry => {
    74	          // Display premium model information if available (Copilot-specific)
    75	          if (!entry.model_info) return "";
    76	
    77	          const modelInfo = entry.model_info;
    78	          let markdown = "";
    79	
    80	          // Display model name and vendor
    81	          if (modelInfo.name) {
    82	            markdown += `**Model Name:** ${modelInfo.name}`;
    83	            if (modelInfo.vendor) {
    84	              markdown += ` (${modelInfo.vendor})`;
    85	            }
    86	            markdown += "\n\n";
    87	          }
    88	
    89	          // Display billing/premium information
    90	          if (modelInfo.billing) {
    91	            const billing = modelInfo.billing;
    92	            if (billing.is_premium === true) {
    93	              markdown += `**Premium Model:** Yes`;
    94	              if (billing.multiplier && billing.multiplier !== 1) {
    95	                markdown += ` (${billing.multiplier}x cost multiplier)`;
    96	              }
    97	              markdown += "\n";
    98	
    99	              if (billing.restricted_to && Array.isArray(billing.restricted_to) && billing.restricted_to.length > 0) {
   100	                markdown += `**Required Plans:** ${billing.restricted_to.join(", ")}\n`;
   101	              }
   102	              markdown += "\n";
   103	            } else if (billing.is_premium === false) {
   104	              markdown += `**Premium Model:** No\n\n`;
   105	            }
   106	          }
   107	
   108	          return markdown;
   109	        },
   110	      }),
   111	  });
   112	
   113	  let markdown = conversationResult.markdown;
   114	
   115	  // Add Information section
   116	  const lastEntry = logEntries[logEntries.length - 1];
   117	  const initEntry = logEntries.find(entry => entry.type === "system" && entry.subtype === "init");
   118	
   119	  markdown += generateInformationSection(lastEntry, {
   120	    additionalInfoCallback: entry => {
   121	      // Display premium request consumption if using a premium model
   122	      const isPremiumModel = initEntry && initEntry.model_info && initEntry.model_info.billing && initEntry.model_info.billing.is_premium === true;

   134	/**
   135	 * Scans log content for tool execution errors and builds a map of failed tools
   136	 * @param {string} logContent - Raw debug log content
   137	 * @returns {Map<string, boolean>} Map of tool IDs/names to error status
   138	 */
   139	function scanForToolErrors(logContent) {
   140	  const toolErrors = new Map();
   141	  const lines = logContent.split("\n");
   142	
   143	  // Track recent tool calls to associate errors with them
   144	  const recentToolCalls = [];
   145	  const MAX_RECENT_TOOLS = 10;
   146	
   147	  for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
   148	    const line = lines[i];
   149	
   150	    // Look for tool_calls in data blocks (not in JSON arguments)
   151	    // Only match if it's in a choices/message context
   152	    if (line.includes('"tool_calls":') && !line.includes('\\"tool_calls\\"')) {
   153	      // Next few lines should contain tool call details
   154	      for (let j = i + 1; j < Math.min(i + 30, lines.length); j++) {
   155	        const nextLine = lines[j];
   156	
   157	        // Extract tool call ID
   158	        const idMatch = nextLine.match(/"id":\s*"([^"]+)"/);
   159	        // Extract function name (not arguments with escaped quotes)
   160	        const nameMatch = nextLine.match(/"name":\s*"([^"]+)"/) && !nextLine.includes('\\"name\\"');
   161	
   162	        if (idMatch) {
   163	          const toolId = idMatch[1];
   164	          // Keep looking for the name
   165	          for (let k = j; k < Math.min(j + 10, lines.length); k++) {
   166	            const nameLine = lines[k];
   167	            const funcNameMatch = nameLine.match(/"name":\s*"([^"]+)"/);
   168	            if (funcNameMatch && !nameLine.includes('\\"name\\"')) {
   169	              const toolName = funcNameMatch[1];
   170	              recentToolCalls.unshift({ id: toolId, name: toolName });
   171	              if (recentToolCalls.length > MAX_RECENT_TOOLS) {
   172	                recentToolCalls.pop();
   173	              }
   174	              break;
   175	            }
   176	          }
   177	        }
   178	      }
   179	    }
   180	
   181	    // Look for error messages
   182	    const errorMatch = line.match(/\[ERROR\].*(?:Tool execution failed|Permission denied|Resource not accessible|Error executing tool)/i);
   183	    if (errorMatch) {
   184	      // Try to extract tool name from error line
   185	      const toolNameMatch = line.match(/Tool execution failed:\s*([^\s]+)/i);
   186	      const toolIdMatch = line.match(/tool_call_id:\s*([^\s]+)/i);
   187	
   188	      if (toolNameMatch) {
   189	        const toolName = toolNameMatch[1];
   190	        toolErrors.set(toolName, true);
   191	        // Also mark by ID if we can find it in recent calls
   192	        const matchingTool = recentToolCalls.find(t => t.name === toolName);
   193	        if (matchingTool) {
   194	          toolErrors.set(matchingTool.id, true);
   195	        }
   196	      } else if (toolIdMatch) {
   197	        toolErrors.set(toolIdMatch[1], true);
   198	      } else if (recentToolCalls.length > 0) {
   199	        // Mark the most recent tool call as failed
   200	        const lastTool = recentToolCalls[0];
   201	        toolErrors.set(lastTool.id, true);
   202	        toolErrors.set(lastTool.name, true);
   203	      }
   204	    }
   205	  }
   206	
   207	  return toolErrors;
   208	}

   228	  if (modelMatch) {
   229	    sessionId = `copilot-${modelMatch[1]}-${Date.now()}`;
   230	  }
   231	
   232	  // Extract premium model info from "Got model info:" JSON block
   233	  // Look for a multi-line JSON block that starts with "Got model info: {" and ends with "}"
   234	  const gotModelInfoIndex = logContent.indexOf("[DEBUG] Got model info: {");
   235	  if (gotModelInfoIndex !== -1) {
   236	    // Find the start of the JSON (the opening brace)
   237	    const jsonStart = logContent.indexOf("{", gotModelInfoIndex);
   238	    if (jsonStart !== -1) {
   239	      // Track braces to find the end of the JSON
   240	      let braceCount = 0;
   241	      let inString = false;
   242	      let escapeNext = false;
   243	      let jsonEnd = -1;
   244	
   245	      for (let i = jsonStart; i < logContent.length; i++) {
   246	        const char = logContent[i];
   247

   249	          escapeNext = false;
   250	          continue;

   253	        if (char === "\\") {
   254	          escapeNext = true;
   255	          continue;
   256	        }
   257	
   258	        if (char === '"' && !escapeNext) {
   259	          inString = !inString;
   260	          continue;

 - Follow security best practices: minimal permissions, explicit network access, no template injection
 - **Network configuration**: Use ecosystem identifiers (`node`, `python`, `go`, etc.) or explicit FQDNs in `network.allowed`. Bare shorthands like `npm` or `pypi` are **not** valid. See https://github.com/github/gh-aw/blob/main/.github/aw/network.md for the full list of valid ecosystem identifiers and domain patterns.
 - **Single-file output**: When creating a workflow, produce exactly **one** workflow `.md` file. Do not create separate documentation files (architecture docs, runbooks, usage guides, etc.). If documentation is needed, add a brief `## Usage` section inside the workflow file itself.
+- **Triggering runs**: Always use `gh aw run <workflow-name>` to trigger a workflow on demand — not `gh workflow run <file>.lock.yml`. `gh aw run` handles workflow resolution by short name, input parsing and validation, and correct run-tracking for agentic workflows. Use `--ref <branch>` to run on a specific branch.
+- **CLI commands reference**: For a complete guide on all `gh aw` commands and their MCP tool equivalents (for restricted environments), see https://github.com/github/gh-aw/blob/main/.github/aw/cli-commands.md

 // extractToolName extracts a tool name from a log line
 func extractToolName(line string) string {
-	// Try to extract tool name from various patterns
-	for _, pattern := range toolNamePatterns {
-		if matches := pattern.FindStringSubmatch(line); len(matches) > 1 {
-			return strings.TrimSpace(matches[1])
+	candidates := []string{strings.TrimSpace(line)}
+	if _, message, ok := strings.Cut(line, "]"); ok {
+		candidates = append(candidates, strings.TrimSpace(message))
+	}
+	if _, message, ok := strings.Cut(line, ":"); ok {
+		candidates = append(candidates, strings.TrimSpace(message))
+	}
+
+	// Try to extract tool name from explicit invocation patterns only.
+	for _, candidate := range candidates {
+		for _, pattern := range toolNamePatterns {
+			if matches := pattern.FindStringSubmatch(candidate); len(matches) > 1 {
+				return strings.TrimSpace(matches[1])
+			}
